(NASDAQ&#58; GOOG, GOOGL) today announced financial results for the quarter ended March&#160;31, 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Sundar Pichai, CEO of Alphabet and Google, said&#58; &#8220;We are pleased with our business performance in the first quarter, with Search performing well and momentum in Cloud. We introduced important product updates anchored in deep computer science and AI. We remain committed to delivering long-term growth and creating capacity to invest in our most compelling growth areas by re-engineering our cost base.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Q1 2023 financial highlights</font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> (unaudited)</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Our first quarter 2023 results reflect&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">i.</font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.01pt">$2.6 billion in charges related to reductions in our workforce and office space&#59; </font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">ii.</font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:10.79pt">a $988 million reduction in depreciation expense from the change in estimated useful life of our servers and certain network equipment&#59; these charges are included within unallocated corporate costs in our segment results.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Change in Useful Lives of Our Server and Network Equipment</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In January 2023, we completed an assessment of the useful lives of our servers and network equipment and adjusted the estimated useful life of our servers from four years to six years and the estimated useful life of certain network equipment from five years to six years. This change in accounting estimate was effective beginning in fiscal year 2023 and the effect for the three months ended March 31, 2023 was a reduction in depreciation expense of $988 million and an increase in net income of $770 million, or $0.06 per basic and $0.06 per diluted share.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Timing of Our Annual Employee Equity Grants</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Beginning in 2023, the timing of our annual employee stock-based compensation awards shifted from January to March. While the shift in timing itself will not affect the amount of stock-based compensation expense over the full fiscal year 2023, it results in relatively less expense recognized in the first quarter compared to the remaining quarters of the year.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Stock Repurchases</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">On April 19, 2023, the Board of Directors of Alphabet authorized the company to repurchase up to an additional $70.0&#160;billion of its Class A and Class C shares in a manner deemed in the best interest of the company and its stockholders, taking into account the economic cost and prevailing market conditions, including the relative trading prices and volumes of the Class A and Class C shares. The repurchases are expected to be executed from time to time, subject to general business and market conditions and other investment opportunities, through open market purchases or privately negotiated transactions, including through Rule 10b5-1 plans.</font></div><div id="ie3f322c14be149d3990b9ff7fa1ac395_7"></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Webcast and conference call information</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A live audio webcast of our first quarter 2023 earnings release call will be available on YouTube at https&#58;&#47;&#47;www.youtube.com&#47;watch&#63;v&#61;76CVRgZUfps. We undertake no duty to update this information unless required by law.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">About non-GAAP financial measures</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">To supplement our consolidated financial statements, which are prepared and presented in accordance with GAAP, we use the following non-GAAP financial measures&#58; free cash flow&#59; constant currency revenues&#59; and percentage change in constant currency revenues. The presentation of this financial information is not intended to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for, or superior to, the financial information prepared and presented in accordance with GAAP.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">We use these non-GAAP financial measures for financial and operational decision-making and as a means to evaluate period-to-period comparisons. We believe that these non-GAAP financial measures provide meaningful supplemental information regarding our performance and liquidity by excluding certain items that may not be indicative of our recurring core business operating results, such as our revenues excluding the effect of foreign exchange rate movements and hedging activities, which are recognized at the consolidated level. We believe that both management and investors benefit from referring to these non-GAAP financial measures in assessing our performance and when planning, forecasting, and analyzing future periods. These non-GAAP financial measures also facilitate management&#8217;s internal comparisons to our historical performance and liquidity as well as comparisons to our competitors&#8217; operating results. We believe these non-GAAP financial measures are useful to investors both because (1) they allow for greater transparency with respect to key metrics used by management in its financial and operational decision-making and (2) they are used by our institutional investors and the analyst community to help them analyze the health of our business.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">There are a number of limitations related to the use of non-GAAP financial measures. We compensate for these limitations by providing specific information regarding the GAAP amounts excluded from these non-GAAP financial measures and evaluating these non-GAAP financial measures together with their relevant financial measures in accordance with GAAP.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For more information on these non-GAAP financial measures, please see the tables captioned style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:40.46pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Reconciliation from GAAP revenues to non-GAAP constant currency revenues and GAAP percentage change in revenues to non-GAAP percentage change in constant currency revenues </font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">(in millions, except percentages&#59; unaudited)</font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">We provide non-GAAP constant currency revenues (&#8220;constant currency revenues&#8221;) and non-GAAP percentage change in constant currency revenues (&#8220;percentage change in constant currency revenues&#8221;), because they facilitate the comparison of current results to historic performance by excluding the effect of foreign exchange rate movements (&#8220;FX Effect&#8221;) as well as hedging activities, which are recognized at the consolidated level, as they are not indicative of our core operating results.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Non-GAAP constant currency revenues is defined as revenues excluding the effect of foreign exchange rate movements and hedging activities and is calculated by translating current period revenues using prior period exchange rates and excluding any hedging effect recognized in the current period. We calculate the percentage change in constant currency revenues by comparing constant currency revenues to the prior year comparable period revenues, excluding any hedging effect recognized in the prior period.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Revenues by Geography</font></div><div
